1. Scan BIN barcode ^KJ6ump7B

We need to configure the BIN properly at this stage
1. Assert BIN is empty as per both WMS and RCS
2. Confirm the BIN layout. 
   2.a Show the current layout if any visually on HT
     2.a.a Worker using the same layout?  continue as normal. DONE
     2.b.b Worker wants to use a different layout?  2x2 --> 1x2 for eg? 
          1.  Reconfigure in UI, save config in WMS , pass it on to RCS too. 
            (technically since this bin is out of OKS, it shouldn't be in RCS)
          2. Confirm the new settings. Save. DONE ^GtjHpptU

WMS/Warehousing
Inbound -> receiving items in warehouse
Outbound--> 


Stow API
 -> what you are putting, and where
   Array[Filled/Empty SKU BIN, tile]  
    - min len 1

Material Movement
- Person brings items to 
OKS Temporary Area
- Worker uses CustomerWMS 
location move to record movement of items 
to OKS Location
- wms_interface sync's this location move 
to OKS inventory, by creating 3 Matching Transactions
of +(positive) inventory count.   ^uQ7mByPY

2.n.2 Item Scan ^WIogO3zr

Scan the Item Barcode. 
   This barcode needs to be matched with JAN code
   Manual Entry should be allowed
Scan Quantity 
   Quantity should be set to 1 by default
   Quantity Increase/Decrease should be allowed. 
   Quantity entry by calculator style UI should be possible.  ^njDpQyKO

2.n For each Item ^PWd243Id

2.n.1 Bin Partition Selection ^H3p8yXpL

We already have selected a BIN. 
We show a UI to select the Bin/Partition where we want to put the items
   - In case the partition layout is set to 1x1 [no partition] skip this step
UI needs to indicate orientation of the bin and the correct way to identify partition. 
Each selection in the UI for a partition, should map to a valid BARCODE(also called LPN) 
  for the specific partition ^2LSyJAFw

2.n.3 Bin or Partition Is FULL ^5QU5PBcs

If Bin is full
    GOTO  Step 1.
If Bin Partition is Full
    GOTO Step 2.n.1

If we don't have any more Items
    BREAK out of For Each Item Loop ^C7mlBqVb

Step 1.
Menu 
Inbound > Stow

Step 2.

 SKU Bin [filled]
 Order Bin [Empty]

Step 3.
Scan Station Barcode
  - laminated, printed, 
  - hung on the structure

Step 4.
Show Tiles available
 - Each Tile shows if you 
   have placed a bin on it

For each Tile
Step 5.n  n < 8
  - Scan Button next to tile. 
  - Scan Bin
  - Scan Tile [to confirm right tile]

Step 6.
Stow button at the end
initiates stow for all
the scanned tiles. 

FIN



 ^GT12KgVo

Incoming Queue
- Configurable Depth - D upto 5
- Total Incoming Tiles on Edge - L [8 eg]
- 1 robot "valet" stationed closed by to aid quick stow
- Stowing done by human in Batches of 8 [function(L)]
- Robot can relatively "quickly"  move 8 bins to the 
  top most empty Depth Level

- Human should be able to place 8 more bins after robot
  is done "staging" previous batch of 8

- This can continue upto 5 time
   ROUND 1 - 8.   Taken to 
FIFO 2D Queue ^6YYvcyPk

TILE Capacity
8 x 6 = 48 
8 x 1 = Active Tiles where human places items
8 x 5 = Stowing queue
